Added 7 new features in `fx.js`:

**1. Digital Rain** — Full-screen Matrix-style katakana/ASCII rain canvas behind all content, respects chaos level for speed and opacity.

**2. Terminal Ops Feed** — Scrolling live log inside the terminal panel with fake cage incident entries (`[INF]`, `[WRN]`, `[ERR]`) every ~2-4 seconds.

**3. Typewriter Effect** — The lead paragraph types itself in character by character on page load with natural punctuation delays.

**4. Scroll Reveal** — Sections (`#mission`, `#ops`, `#signals`, `#contact`, `.showcase`) fade and slide up as they enter the viewport.

**5. Mouse Glow Trail** — A large colored radial gradient that follows the cursor, cycling hue based on chaos level — makes the whole page feel alive.

**6. Konami Code Easter Egg** — Type ↑↑↓↓←→←→BA to unleash maximum chaos: hue cycling every 1.2s, flashing rainbow banner, and a special terminal entry.

**7. Web Audio Ambient** — Low 38Hz/52Hz drone with random high-frequency beeps, activates on first user interaction. Adds subtle cyberpunk atmosphere.

All effects tie into the `--editor-chaos` variable so the live edit commands (`more chaos`, `calm mode`, etc.) control them too.

For the 3D scene, I need to add a hamster and wheel. Let me think about the geometry:
- Wheel: TorusGeometry, but actually for a hamster wheel it's a flat disc with rungs. A simpler approach: a torus with very thin radius. Or just a cylinder rotating. Let me use a cylinder with spokes.

Actually, the simplest: a torus + a small sphere/box that orbits on it (the hamster). The wheel rotates around its own axis, and the hamster sits on top and bobs.

Let me code:
```js
const wheelGroup = new THREE.Group();
wheelGroup.position.set(0, 0.8, 1.0);
rig.add(wheelGroup);

// Wheel: thin torus
const wheel = new THREE.Mesh(
  new THREE.TorusGeometry(0.32, 0.03, 8, 32),
  materials.rack
);
wheel.rotation.y = Math.PI / 2; // facing sideways
wheelGroup.add(wheel);

// Rungs
for (let i = 0; i < 6; i++) {
  const angle = (i / 6) * Math.PI * 2;
  const rung = new THREE.Mesh(
    new THREE.CylinderGeometry(0.015, 0.015, 0.06, 6),
    materials.cableCyan
  );
  rung.position.set(0, Math.sin(angle) * 0.32, Math.cos(angle) * 0.32);
  rung.rotation.x = angle;
  wheelGroup.add(rung);
}

// Hamster (small sphere on the wheel)
const hamster = new THREE.Mesh(
  new THREE.SphereGeometry(0.08, 12, 12),
  new THREE.MeshStandardMaterial({ color: 0xd2a36b, roughness: 0.6 })
);
hamster.position.set(0, 0.32, 0);
wheelGroup.add(hamster);
```

Then in the animation loop:
```js
wheel.rotation.z += 0.06 * chaos;
// hamster bobs with the rotation
hamster.position.y = 0.32 * Math.cos(wheel.rotation.z);
hamster.position.x = 0.32 * Math.sin(wheel.rotation.z);
```

That should give a hamster running on a wheel effect.

persistAndReport(changes) {\n+    applyState();\n+    const shared = await saveSharedState();\n+    say(\"bot\", `Applied: ${[...new Set(changes)].join(\", \")}. ${shared ? \"Saved for everyone.\" : \"Saved locally only.\"}`);\n+  }\n+\n+  async function applyPrompt(raw) {\n+    const prompt = raw.trim();\n+    const text = prompt.toLowerCase();\n+    const changes = [];\n+\n+    if (!prompt) return;\n+    say(\"user\", prompt);\n+\n+    if (text.includes(\"reset\")) {\n+      state = { ...defaults };\n+      changes.push(\"reset the page to defaults\");\n+    }\n+\n+    const title = extractAfter(prompt, [\"title \", \"headline \", \"h1 \"]);\n+    if (title) {\n+      state.title = title;\n+      changes.push(\"changed the headline\");\n+    }\n+\n+    const lead = extractAfter(prompt, [\"lead \", \"subtitle \", \"description \"]);\n+    if (lead) {\n+      state.lead = lead;\n+      changes.push(\"changed the intro text\");\n+    }\n+\n+    const banner = extractAfter(prompt, [\"banner \", \"alert \", \"announcement \"]);\n+    if (banner) {\n+      state.banner = banner;\n+      changes.push(\"added a live banner\");\n+    }\n+\n+    if (text.includes(\"hide banner\") || text.includes(\"remove banner\")) {\n+      state.banner = \"\";\n+      changes.push(\"removed the banner\");\n+    }\n+\n+    if (text.includes(\"chaos\") || text.includes(\"crazy\") || text.includes(\"insane\") || text.includes(\"more animation\")) {\n+      state.chaos = Math.min(3, Number(state.chaos || defaults.chaos) + 0.65);\n+      changes.push(\"increased animation intensity\");\n+    }\n+\n+    if (text.includes(\"calm\") || text.includes(\"less\") || text.includes(\"quiet\")) {\n+      state.chaos = Math.max(0.25, Number(state.chaos || defaults.chaos) - 0.75);\n+      changes.push(\"reduced animation intensity\");\n+    }\n+\n+    if (text.includes(\"matrix\") || text.includes(\"green\")) state.hue = \"green\";\n+    if (text.includes(\"red\") || text.includes(\"alarm\") || text.includes(\"incident\")) state.hue = \"red\";\n+    if (text.includes(\"blue\") || text.includes(\"ice\")) state.hue = \"blue\";\n+    if (text.includes(\"purple\") || text.includes(\"violet\")) state.hue = \"purple\";\n+    if (text.includes(\"amber\") || text.includes(\"orange\") || text.includes(\"gold\")) state.hue = \"amber\";\n+\n+    if (text.includes(\"night mode\") || text.includes(\"dark mode\") || text.includes(\" bedtime\") || text.includes(\"lights off\")) {\n+      state.time = \"night\";\n+      changes.push(\"switched the cage to night cycle\");\n+    }\n+\n+    if (text.includes(\"day mode\") || text.includes(\"lights on\") || text.includes(\" morning\") || text.includes(\"sunrise\")) {\n+      state.time = \"day\";\n+      changes.push(\"switched the cage to day cycle\");\n+    }\n+\n+    if ([\"green\", \"red\", \"blue\", \"purple\", \"amber\"].some((color) => text.includes(color)) || text.includes(\"matrix\") || text.includes(\"alarm\")) {\n+      changes.push(`switched theme to ${state.hue}`);\n+    }\n+\n+    if (!changes.length) {\n+      state.banner = prompt;\n+      state.chaos = Math.min(3, Number(state.chaos || defaults.chaos) + 0.2);\n+      changes.push(\"posted your text as a live banner\");\n+    }\n+\n+    await persistAndReport(changes);\n+  }\n+\n+  async function setSharedPatch(patch, label) {\n+    state = { ...state, ...patch };\n+    applyState();\n+    const shared = await saveSharedState();\n+    if (label) say(\"bot\", `${label} ${shared ? \"Saved for everyone.\" : \"Saved locally only.\"}`);\n+  }\n+\n+  window.c3cockEditor = {\n+    getState: () => ({ ...state }),\n+    setState: (patch, label) => setSharedPatch(patch, label),\n+    setTime: (time) => setSharedPatch({ time }, `Switched to ${time} cycle.`),\n+  };\n+\n+  toggle.addEventListener(\"click\", () => {\n+    const closed = applyPrompt(input.value);\n+    input.value = \"\";\n+  });\n+\n+  document.querySelectorAll(\"[data-prompt]\").forEach((button) => {\n+    button.addEventListener(\"click\", () => defaults\"]);\n+  });\n+\n+  async function pollSharedState() {\n+    if (saving) return;\n+    try {\n+      const shared = await loadSharedState();\n+      if (!shared.updatedAt || shared.updatedAt === lastSeenUpdatedAt) return;\n+\n+      const before = JSON.stringify(stripMeta(state));\n+      const after = JSON.stringify(stripMeta(shared));\n+      state = { ...defaults, ...shared };\n+      lastSeenUpdatedAt = shared.updatedAt;\n+      saveLocalState(state);\n+\n+      if (before !== after) {\n+        applyState();\n+        say(\"bot\", \"Synced shared edits from another visitor.\");\n+      }\n+    } catch {\n+      // Keep the last known state if polling fails.\n+    }\n+  }\n+\n+  async function boot() {\n+    try {\n+      state = await loadSharedState();\n+      lastSeenUpdatedAt = state.updatedAt || \"\";\n+      saveLocalState(state);\n+      applyState();\n+      say(\"bot\", \"Shared editor online. Changes now persist for every visitor.\");\n+    } catch {\n+      state = loadLocalState();\n+      applyState();\n+      say(\"bot\", \"Shared editor API is offline; using local edits until it returns.\");\n+      warnedOffline = true;\n+    }\n+\n+    setInterval(pollSharedState, 5000);\n+  }\n+\n+  boot();\n+})();\n*** End Patch"

What it does:
- Adds `GET /api/state` and `POST /api/state`
- Stores shared editor state on disk in `data/editor-state.json`
- Chat edits now persist for all users
- Other visitors sync changes automatically every 5 seconds
- Day/night toggle also saves globally
- API only accepts sanitized fields: `title`, `lead`, `banner`, `chaos`, `hue`, `time`

I did **not** expose public `opencode` execution. That would let anyone on the internet run server-side edits/commands. This is the safer persistent version.
